 ) Cumin, which is hot, but has many benefits according to health
 sabji, daal, raite main tadake se lekar kai deshi dawaaiyon main iskaa istemaal hota he, lekin kya aapako pataa he bazaar main nakli jira aa rahaa he
 This fake cumin is fatal in terms of health
 bataa den, dilli police ne bavana ilaake main ek aisi hi factory kaa bhandaphod kiya he jahaan nakli jira ban rahaa tha
 The police have recovered 19,500 kilograms of fake cumin, which was being prepared from grass, stone dust and sugar molasses
 dilli ke bavana ilaake main ek nakli zeera banane vaali factory kaa bhandaphod,kareeb 19400 kilo nakli zeera baraamad,factory maalik samet 5 giraftaar,ghaas,pathar ke powder or shire se banataa tha zeera ,swasthya ke liye behad hanikaarak,aise banaate the jaanaleva zeera pic
 twitter
 com / nd03h4wdmxbahari uttari dilli ke disipi gaurav sharma ke mutabik unki team ko jaankaree mili ki bavana ke pooth khurd gaanv main ek factory main nakli jira banaaya ja rahaa he
 When the police raided the factory with the team of FSO and FSSI, a total of 5 people were arrested, including factory owner Harinandan and 4 laborers
 factory main kul 19400 kilo nakli jira, 5250 kilo pathar kaa buraada, 1600 kilo ghaas or 1225 kilo jira baraamad hua
 Accused Harinandan said that he is a resident of Jalalabad village of Shahjahanpur
 nakli jira banane kaa kaam usne apane gaanv main se hi siikhaa
 He hired a warehouse job in Bawana in the month of August this year and then started making fake cumin
 nakli jira banane ke liye kaccha maal wo rajasthan se maangata tha
 He told that first of all special kind is added to molasses, then mix the powder of stone and fake cumin is prepared
 police ke mutabik ye jaharila jira 20 rupee kilo main vyapaariyon ko diya jaataa he
 Traders mix and sell this fake cumin in real cumin
 milawat aisi kii jaati he ki 20 pratishat nakli or 80 pratishat asli jira ho
 So that people do not know about food
 bazaar main asli jire kii keemat kareeb 400 rupee kilo he
 In the factory, the laborers used to get 2 rupees for making 1 kg of cumin
 is jire kii supplai uttar pradesh or rajasthan main kii ja rahi thi
 According to doctors, this poisonous cumin can cause serious diseases related to kidney and liver, which are fatal

 What is loan write-off? npas of banks carry loans given to the corporate sector
 bank se liye gaye karj par jab companiyaan byaaj tak nahin chukaa paati or bank kaa mul dhan duubataa dikhaai dene lagata he to ukt karj ko bank enpie (non parforming asset) qaraar detaa he

 Pressure cooker is the most important utensil of cooking utensils, after closing the lid, you do not need to move a spoon nor check whether the food is cooked or not
 bas siti ke hisaab se andaja lag jaataa he ki khaanaa taiyaar he
 However, there are some problems and dilemmas with it too
 inhen ko dur karne kaa tarika ham aapako yahaan bataa rahe hai:- kookar se pani baahar anakai baar aisa hota he ki pressure kookar se pani baahar nikal aata he or yah itnaa garm hota he ki sharir par pade iske chhinton se twachaa laal ho jaati he
 The reason for this is not the ratio of the amount of water in the pressure cooker
 khaane kii tulana main pani zyada ho tokukar se pani baahar nikalataa he
 By doing this, the food also becomes tasteless
 isse bachane ke liye pani kii maatra kaa sahi andaja lagaana seekhen
 - Everything does not boil in the cooker
 Many people boil everything in the pressure cooker
 jabaki har cheez kshapana rup or pakane kaa apana tarika hotahai
 Cereals and some vegetables can be boiled in the cooker, but not everything
 - masaalon kaa galat istemalpressure kookar main khaanaa banane ke dauraan log masaalon ke istemaal par dhyaan nahin dete
 If you want your food to be delicious, then use fresh vegetables and fresh spices
 agar ye sambhav na ho to khadey masaalon kaa prayog karen
 - Keep onion in the use of garlic
 Many times people put raw onion, garlic and ginger in the pressure cooker during cooking
 lekin isse khaane kaa swaad nahin aata
 While cooking in a cooker, it would be better to fry onion, garlic and ginger in a frying pan first
 aisa karne se in chizon kii mahak va swaad barkaraar rahenge
